beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(18)
      debugLogForScript: s32'312', 0, 0
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg7), Val(1)
      findState: s32'cmn_AfroObj', 11, 2, 52
      isObjectActive: (STACK7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK7)
          setObjectWidth: 1000
          setObjectHeight: 900
          setObjectDepth: 750
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_SLY', 2, 157
  if: Mem(TrainingValue)
    if: Mem(IsRecoverableTypeA)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(360)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(2)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(3)
    setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 1500, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(3)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(0)
    setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 0, 16
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerDamage)
      ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
        ifOperation: (PERCENT), Val(50), Val(100)
          sendValuesToObject: 0, 0, 0, 0
          createObjectWithArg: s32'SLY_010_bat_move', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          sendValuesToObject: 0, 1, 0, 0
          createObjectWithArg: s32'SLY_010_bat_move', (PLAYER)
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    isObjectActive: (STACK0)
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      if: Mem(BattleDoing)
        createObject: s32'SLY_409_aura', (PLAYER)
        stackObject: (STACK0), (PREVIOUS)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(BattleDoing)
      ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
        ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
          ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
            if: Mem(IsNeutral)
              modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(-1)
            endIf: 
            else: 
              ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
                modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(-1)
              endIf: 
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifNotInObject: (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(Timeup)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnGuard'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnGuard'
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal6), Val(0)
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnDamage'

beginSubroutine: s32'OnActionBeginPre'
  checkMoveFlag: (DEBUG)
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Check', Mem(AdjustmentForScript0), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnActionBegin'
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFWalk'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBWalk'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActAirFDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActAirBDash'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActJumpPre'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_ResetRedRCTime'
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(PlayerVal7)
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(2)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActJumpPre'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(2)
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFinalize'
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'sly_SP_03'
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'sly_SP_04'
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'CoatReset'
  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Val(0)
  setCmnMaterialParam: 19, 0, 0
  sendSignalToAction: s32'SLY_010_bat_move', (SIGNAL1)
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'CmnActFDash'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'CmnFDash'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      setCommonActionMark: 1
      enableBurst: 1
      enableRomanCancelMove: 1
      upon: (IDLING)
        addTensionValAtMoveBBS: 12
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(1)
          displayModel: 0
          enableJump: 1
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1)
          sendSignalToAction: s32'SLY_010_bat_move', (SIGNAL0)
          createObject: s32'SLY_Step_Start', (PLAYER)
          createObject: s32'SLY_Step_Start_bat', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(7)
          setNoCollision: 0
          enableJump: 0
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
          physicsXImpulse: 0, 60000
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(12)
          setNoCollision: 1
          physicsXImpulse: 0, 0
          faceOpponent: 
          createObject: s32'SLY_Step_End_reverse', (PLAYER)
          createObject: s32'SLY_Step_End_bat', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(18)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Cancel_FDash'
  gotoLabelIf: s32'Cancel_FDash', Mem(Tmp)
  sprite: s32'sly000_00ex', 30
  sprite: s32'sly000_00', 2147483647
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'end'
  beginLabel: s32'Cancel_FDash'
  sprite: s32'sly000_00ex', 30
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnFDashCancel'
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
  upon: (IDLING)
    addTensionValAtMoveBBS: 12
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(1)
      displayModel: 0
      sendSignalToAction: s32'SLY_010_bat_move', (SIGNAL0)
      createObject: s32'SLY_Step_Start', (PLAYER)
      createObject: s32'SLY_Step_Start_bat', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(3)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (BEFORE_EXIT)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(7)
      setNoCollision: 0
      physicsXImpulse: 0, 40000
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(18)
      setNoCollision: 1
      physicsXImpulse: 0, 0
      faceOpponent: 
      createObject: s32'SLY_Step_End', (PLAYER)
      createObject: s32'SLY_Step_End_bat', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(26)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'sly000_00', 2147483647
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'end'
  jumpToState: s32'_NEUTRAL'
endState:

beginSubroutine: s32'BloodFunc'
  if: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    upon: (HIT)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (HIT)
      if: Mem(BattleDoing)
        ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
          ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyPlayerDown)
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
            callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_hittype_universe', Val(0), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
            createObject: s32'sharon_universe', (PLAYER)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Master_Wait'
